<h1 _ngcontent-rmj-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.wifiManager (WLAN)"> @ohos.wifiManager (WLAN) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>该模块主要提供WLAN基础功能（无线接入、无线加密、无线漫游等）、P2P（peer-to-peer）服务的基础功能和WLAN消息通知的相应服务，让应用可以通过WLAN和其他设备互联互通。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 9开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="hljs-string">'@kit.ConnectivityKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1100px;">     <h2 id="wifimanageriswifiactive9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.isWifiActive<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanageriswifiactive9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>isWifiActive(): boolean</p>     <p>查询WLAN开关是否已使能。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">true:已使能， false:未使能。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1039px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagerenablewifi15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.enableWifi<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagerenablewifi15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableWifi(): void</p>     <p>启动WLAN。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO 和 (ohos.permission.MANAGE_WIFI_CONNECTION 仅系统应用可用 或 ohos.permission.MANAGE_ENTERPRISE_WIFI_CONNECTION 仅企业应用可用)</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.disableWifi<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon 仅系统应用可用 或 ohos.permission.MANAGE_ENTERPRISE_WIFI_CONNECTION 仅企业应用可用)</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> <h2 id="wifimanagerscan9deprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.scan<sup>9+</sup><sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagerscan9deprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>scan(): void</p>     <p>启动WLAN扫描，使用前先使能WLAN。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从 API version 9开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃。建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanagerstartscan21">wifiManager.startScan</a>代替。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO、ohos.permission.LOCATION 和 ohos.permission.APPROXIMATELY_LOCATION</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> 1072px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagerstartscan21" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.startScan<sup>21+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagerstartscan21" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>startScan(): void</p>     <p>启动WLAN扫描。</p>     <ul>      <li>应用程序在前台运行时，两分钟内最多可扫描四次。</li>      <li>在后台运行时，三十分钟内最多可扫描一次。</li>      <li>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanageronwifiscanstatechange9">on('wifiScanStateChange')</a>订阅扫描状态变更事件，监听扫描完成通知。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码说明文档</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 990px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetscanresults9deprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getScanResults<sup>9+</sup><sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetscanresults9deprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getScanResults(): Promise&lt;Array&lt;WifiScanInfo&gt;&gt;</p>     <p>获取扫描结果，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <ul>      <li>返回一个Promise对象，解析后得到一个包含多个WifiScanInfo对象的数组，每个对象表示一个WLAN网络的扫描信息。</li>     </ul>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从 API version 9开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃。建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanagergetscaninfolist10">wifiManager.getScanInfoList</a>代替。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO 和 (ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC 或(ohos.permission.LOCATION 和 ohos.permission.APPROXIMATELY_LOCATION))</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt; Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifiscaninfo9">WifiScanInfo</a>&gt; &gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。返回扫描到的热点列表。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2115px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetscanresults9deprecated-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getScanResults<sup>9+</sup><sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getScanResults(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Array&lt;WifiScanInfo&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>获取扫描结果，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <ul>      <li>通过回调函数返回一个包含多个WifiScanInfo对象的数组，每个对象表示一个WLAN网络的扫描信息。</li>     </ul>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从 API version 9开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃。建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanagergetscaninfolist10">wifiManager.getScanInfoList</a>代替。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO 和 (ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC 或 (ohos.permission.LOCATION 和 ohos.permission.APPROXIMATELY_LOCATION))</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt; Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifiscaninfo9">WifiScanInfo</a>&gt;&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当成功时，err为0，data为扫描到的热点；否则err为非0值，data为空。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> id="wifimanagergetscaninfolist10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getScanInfoList<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetscaninfolist10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getScanInfoList(): Array&lt;WifiScanInfo&gt;</p>     <p>获取包含当前时间点前30s内的缓存扫描结果。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifiscaninfo9">WifiScanInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回扫描到的热点列表。如果应用申请了ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC权限，则返回结果中的bssid为真实设备地址，否则为随机设备地址。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> <p>当securityType为WIFI_SEC_TYPE_WEP时，该字段长度只允许为5、10、13、26、16和32字节其中之一，并且当字段长度为偶数时，该字段必须为纯十六进制数字构成。</p>          <p>当securityType为WIFI_SEC_TYPE_SAE时，该字段最小长度为1字节。</p>          <p>当securityType为WIFI_SEC_TYPE_PSK时，该字段最小长度为8字节。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" <li>包含EAP认证方式、第二阶段认证方式、身份信息、密码、证书等配置项。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> 1849px;">     <h2 id="wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.addCandidateConfig<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addCandidateConfig(config: WifiDeviceConfig): Promise&lt;number&gt;</p>     <p>添加候选网络配置，使用Promise异步回调，使用前先使能WLAN。</p>     <ul>      <li>通过传入<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifideviceconfig9">WifiDeviceConfig</a>对象，配置WLAN网络的详细信息，如SSID、密码、安全类型等。</li>      <li>返回一个Promise对象，解析后得到一个数字，表示配置的ID(用于区分、管理不同WLAN配置，其他相关API操作，错误处理调试等)。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">config</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifideviceconfig9">WifiDeviceConfig</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">WLAN配置信息。如果bssidType未指定值，则bssidType默认为随机设备地址类型。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。表示网络配置ID。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"    }</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1819px;">     <h2 id="wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.addCandidateConfig<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addCandidateConfig(config: WifiDeviceConfig, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>添加候选网络配置，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <ul>      <li>将指定的WLAN设备配置添加为候选网络，添加后的网络在没有连接记录的情况下无法触发自动回连，可以通过 connectToCandidateConfig或connectToCandidateConfigWithUserAction 方法实现候选网络连接，页面确认连接成功后，可实现自动回连。</li>      <li>候选网络属于应用维度添加的网络配置，和系统网络配置是相互隔离的，在系统WLAN页面不可见。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">config</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifideviceconfig9">WifiDeviceConfig</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">WLAN配置信息。如果bssidType未指定值，则bssidType默认为随机设备地址类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>回调函数。err为0时：操作成功，data为添加的网络配置ID，如果data值为-1，表示添加失败。</p>          <p>err为非0值时：操作出现错误。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>Invalid parameters. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified.</p>          <p>2. Incorrect parameter types. 3. Parameter verification failed.</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { wifiManager } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ConnectivityKit'</span>;</li><li>

device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.removeCandidateConfig<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagerremovecandidateconfig9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span <li>从系统中删除指定网络ID的WLAN候选配置，清理不再需要的WLAN候选配置，释放系统资源。</li>      <li>只能移除通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9">addCandidateConfig</a>添加的候选配置，移除后该候选网络将不再被系统自动连接。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>    </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1586px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagerremovecandidateconfig9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.removeCandidateConfig<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span <li>从系统中删除指定网络ID的WLAN候选配置，清理不再需要的WLAN候选配置，释放系统资源。</li>      <li>只能移除通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanageraddcandidateconfig9">addCandidateConfig</a>添加的候选配置，移除后该候选网络将不再被系统自动连接。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.9.1.5.1.1"    </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder"  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1922px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagerconnecttocandidateconfigwithuseraction20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.connectToCandidateConfigWithUserAction<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagerconnecttocandidateconfigwithuseraction20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>connectToCandidateConfigWithUserAction(networkId: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>该接口用于应用连接到用户添加的候选网络，并在连接时提示用户进行信任确认。使用Promise异步回调用户响应结果。</p>     <ul>      <li>调用此接口时，系统将提示用户确认是否信任并连接到指定的候选网络，通过Promise异步返回用户响应结果。</li>      <li>用户确认是连接过程中的必要步骤，未获得用户信任确认前，连接操作不会执行。</li>      <li>建议在发起连接前先通过startScan接口触发一次WLAN扫描，通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanageronwifiscanstatechange9">wifiManager.on('wifiScanStateChange')</a>方法监听到扫描结果刷新后再连接，以提高连接成功率。</li>     </ul>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifimanagerconnecttocandidateconfig9">wifiManager.connectToCandidateConfig</a>连接候选网络时，不会返回用户响应结果。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.SET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1001px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetlinkedinfo9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getLinkedInfo<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetlinkedinfo9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getLinkedInfo(): Promise&lt;WifiLinkedInfo&gt;</p>     <p>获取WLAN连接信息。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO 。</p>     <p>当macType是1 - 设备MAC地址时，获取 macAddress 还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，macAddress 返回随机MAC地址。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifilinkedinfo9">WifiLinkedInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。表示WLAN连接信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1521px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetlinkedinfo9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getLinkedInfo<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetlinkedinfo9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getLinkedInfo(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;WifiLinkedInfo&gt;): void</p>     <p>获取WLAN连接信息。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO 。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当macType是1（设备MAC地址），获取macAddress还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，macAddress返回为空。</li>        <li>如果应用申请了ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC权限，则返回结果中的bssid为真实BSSID地址，否则为随机设备地址。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifilinkedinfo9">WifiLinkedInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当获取成功时，err为0，data表示WLAN连接信息。如果err为非0，表示处理出现错误。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p> width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified. 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Wi-Fi STA disabled.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { wifiManager } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ConnectivityKit'</span>;</li><li>

style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1366px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetlinkedinfosync18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getLinkedInfoSync<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetlinkedinfosync18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getLinkedInfoSync(): WifiLinkedInfo;</p>     <p>获取WLAN连接信息，使用同步方式返回结果。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO 。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当macType是1（设备MAC地址），获取macAddress还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，macAddress返回为空。</li>        <li>如果应用申请了ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC权限，则返回结果中的bssid为真实BSSID地址，否则为随机设备地址。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifilinkedinfo9">WifiLinkedInfo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示WLAN连接信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2501001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Wi-Fi STA disabled.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-rmj-c106=""           </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1203px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagerisconnected9" <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 898px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetp2plinkedinfo9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getP2pLinkedInfo<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetp2plinkedinfo9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getP2pLinkedInfo(): Promise&lt;WifiP2pLinkedInfo&gt;</p>     <p>获取P2P连接信息。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p>获取 groupOwnerAddr 还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，groupOwnerAddr 返回全零地址。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.P2P</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.58.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.58.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifip2plinkedinfo9">WifiP2pLinkedInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。表示P2P连接信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.58.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.58.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2801000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1454px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetp2plinkedinfo9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getP2pLinkedInfo<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetp2plinkedinfo9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getP2pLinkedInfo(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;WifiP2pLinkedInfo&gt;): void</p>     <p>获取P2P连接信息。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p>获取 groupOwnerAddr 还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，groupOwnerAddr 返回全零地址。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.P2P</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifip2plinkedinfo9">WifiP2pLinkedInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当操作成功时，err为0，data表示P2P连接信息。如果err为非0，表示处理出现错误。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifip2pdevice9">WifiP2pDevice[]</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当操作成功时，err为0，data表示对端设备列表信息。如果err为非0，表示处理出现错误。如果应用申请了ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC权限，则返回结果中的deviceAddress为真实设备地址，否则为随机设备地址。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1390px;">     <h2 id="wifimanagergetmultilinkedinfo18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.getMultiLinkedInfo<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanagergetmultilinkedinfo18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当macType是1（设备MAC地址），获取macAddress还需申请ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_LOCAL_MAC权限（该权限仅系统应用可申请），无该权限时，macAddress返回为空。</li>        <li>如果应用申请了ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_PEERS_MAC权限，则返回结果中的bssid为真实BSSID地址，否则为随机设备地址。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-wifimanager#wifilinkedinfo9">WifiLinkedInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Wi-Fi连接信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> id="wifimanageronwifistatechange9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.on('wifiStateChange')<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanageronwifistatechange9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: 'wifiStateChange', callback: Callback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册WLAN状态改变事件，在业务退出时，要调用off(type: 'wifiStateChange', callback?: Callback&lt;number&gt;)接口去掉之前的注册回调。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div        <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td <h2 id="wifimanageronwifiscanstatechange9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wifiManager.on('wifiScanStateChange')<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wifimanageronwifiscanstatechange9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: 'wifiScanStateChange', callback: Callback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>注册扫描状态改变事件，在业务退出时，要调用off(type: 'wifiScanStateChange', callback?: Callback&lt;number&gt;)接口去掉之前的注册回调。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.GET_WIFI_INFO</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Communication.WiFi.STA</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">固定填"wifiScanStateChange"字符串。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">状态改变回调函数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>扫描状态改变事件的枚举：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">枚举值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">扫描失败。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">扫描成功。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">状态改变回调函数。如果callback不填，将取消注册该事件关联的所有回调函数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-wifi">WIFI错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Capability not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2801000</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Operation failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rmj-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { wifiManager } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ConnectivityKit'</span>;</li><li>  </li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">recvP2pDiscoveryChangeFunc</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">result:<span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) =&gt;
